scene_synopsis: "Sunnyside neighborhood has seen better days- its fate is sadly connected to Perfekto Polymers. The townhouses and apartments were built to house the factory workers office staff. Suddenly, five years ago, one of the big eight Megacorporations was interested in the little company, and all of the employees were excited. A corporate VP from Aztechnology even showed up to look over the books and check out the operation.  Then, suddenly the headhunter was gone, with rumors that he had been killed. The CEO died of a heart attack the same night.  Every executive started trying to find work at other companies before the tale of their failure got out. Inside 48 hours, the company was done.\n\nThis was bad news for the employees who showed up on Monday morning, only to learn that they were all out of a job. Since the executives had spent the entire weekend getting new jobs and blaming each other; no one was sure who was to blame, and so no one wanted to hire any of these possibly toxic assets. Only the first few employees managed to sell their homes for anything resembling their actual value, the rest were stranded. Overnight, the neighborhood became a wasteland. "
